  <td style="vertical-align:top; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif; font-weight:bold; padding:.3em 0em 0em 0em; text-shadow: 1px -1px gray;">“</td>
  <td style="padding:1em 1em; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif;; font-style:italic; font-size:medium; color:inherit;">As long as humanity divides itself into factions, no organization in this world can be perfect...! Make assumptions and the enemy will slip up through your grasp! Don't be taken in by appearances!</td>
  <td style="vertical-align:bottom; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif; font-weight:bold; padding-bottom:0em; padding-left:0em; padding-right:0em; text-shadow: -1px 1px gray;">”</td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>
<table style="padding-right: 2%; font-size:80%; text-align:right; width:100%;">
 <tbody><tr valign="top">
  <td><cite style="font-family:&#39;Arial&#39;,sans-serif;">—&#160;Smoker to his G-5 soldiers<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup></cite>
  </td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>

<p><br />
Smoker is merciless against pirates, usually taking a straightforward but efficient approach in capturing them. He is dedicated to the pursuit of global justice against criminals, and never forgets those who forsake the law and manage to escape his grasp, though he recognizes that not all Marines are as noble as their image suggests, nor should all allies be trusted blindly. Smoker holds a rather cynical worldview that makes him question even the Marines, considering the existence of traitors within their ranks a likely possibility. He also does not trust the <a href="/wiki/Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea" title="Seven Warlords of the Sea">Seven Warlords of the Sea</a> despite their status as employees of the <a href="/wiki/World_Government" title="World Government">World Government</a>, as he believes them to be nothing more than pirates (according to him, "once a pirate, always a pirate"), meaning that Smoker rarely leaves them to their own devices.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> This is exacerbated by the fact that Smoker has confronted no less than four different warlords for various reasons, often for knowing too much about their machinations.
</p><p>Smoker tends to hold grudges toward pirates who have escaped him, to the point of ignoring other notable pirates in his way. For example, he recognized <a href="/wiki/Portgas_D._Ace" title="Portgas D. Ace">Portgas D. Ace</a>, a member of the <a href="/wiki/Whitebeard_Pirates" title="Whitebeard Pirates">Whitebeard Pirates</a>, and was ready to confront him in battle, but after <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a> unexpectedly interrupted them, Smoker barely acknowledged Ace's presence and started chasing the Straw Hat captain, who he considers his primary target ever since their scuffle at <a href="/wiki/Loguetown" title="Loguetown">Loguetown</a>. It is worth noting that Smoker's interest in Luffy goes deeper than just that; Smoker has witnessed parallels between <a href="/wiki/Gol_D._Roger" title="Gol D. Roger">Gold Roger</a> and the young pirate, such as a <a href="/wiki/Will_of_D." title="Will of D.">defiant smile</a> in the face of death as well as seemingly miraculous luck.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d5/Smoker_Stacking_Stones.png/revision/latest?cb=20220628173819" class="image"><img alt="Smoker Stacking Stones" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="222" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Smoker Stacking Stones.png" data-image-key="Smoker_Stacking_Stones.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d5/Smoker_Stacking_Stones.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220628173819" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d5/Smoker_Stacking_Stones.png/revision/latest?cb=20220628173819" class="image"><img alt="Smoker Stacking Stones" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d5/Smoker_Stacking_Stones.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220628173819" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="222" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Smoker Stacking Stones.png" data-image-key="Smoker_Stacking_Stones.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d5/Smoker_Stacking_Stones.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220628173819" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Smoker_Stacking_Stones.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Smoker stacking stones as entertainment.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As can be deduced from his name, Smoker is an avid smoker, almost never being seen without at least one cigar on his mouth. He is such a habitual smoker that he continues smoking even when wearing a gas mask. He also instinctively prefers to walk around with his chest bare, doing so even after having his mind transferred to the body of a woman. Smoker seems to have a hobby in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rock_balancing" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Rock balancing">rock balancing</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-intro_3-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-intro-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> As such, he does not seem to like when people make too much noise around him, as he claims that it breaks his focus.<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup><br style="clear:both;" />
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Relationships">Relationships</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSmoker%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D8&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Marines">Marines</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSmoker%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D9&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Smoker's reputation among the Marines is rather notorious, although not entirely in a positive manner. This generally stems from his disrespectful attitude, problematic history, and intimidating looks. For those reasons, civilians and even some lower-ranked Marines can become nervous at his presence, especially when he starts berating them.<sup id="cite_ref-intro_3-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-intro-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Smoker is not afraid to openly challenge the higher-ranking echelons within the Marines or the <a href="/wiki/World_Government" title="World Government">World Government</a>, going as far as to use a brutal insult in an attempt to reject a promotion that he did not want, showing no fear for any potential backlash.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Tashigi">Tashigi</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSmoker%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D10&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Smoker has a close relationship with his subordinate <a href="/wiki/Tashigi" title="Tashigi">Tashigi</a>, who is always dutifully at his side. Tashigi is a protégé of Smoker. However, he appears to react very harshly to her mistakes (usually caused by her clumsiness or poor vision) and sometimes thinks of her as a sorry excuse for a soldier.<sup id="cite_ref-intro_3-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-intro-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> Despite this, Smoker has shown that he trusts her judgment, encouraging her to just follow her own sense of justice in times of doubt. When Smoker needs to absent himself during a mission, he puts Tashigi in charge of his other subordinates, also putting trust in her strength. 
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 200px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/5e/Tashigi_Cries_For_Smoker%27s_Encouragement.png/revision/latest?cb=20230316020342" class="image"><img alt="Tashigi Cries For Smoker&#39;s Encouragement" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="150" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Tashigi Cries For Smoker&#39;s Encouragement.png" data-image-key="Tashigi_Cries_For_Smoker%27s_Encouragement.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/5e/Tashigi_Cries_For_Smoker%27s_Encouragement.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230316020342" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/5e/Tashigi_Cries_For_Smoker%27s_Encouragement.png/revision/latest?cb=20230316020342" class="image"><img alt="Tashigi Cries For Smoker&#39;s Encouragement" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/5e/Tashigi_Cries_For_Smoker%27s_Encouragement.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230316020342" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="150" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Tashigi Cries For Smoker&#39;s Encouragement.png" data-image-key="Tashigi_Cries_For_Smoker%27s_Encouragement.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/5e/Tashigi_Cries_For_Smoker%27s_Encouragement.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230316020342" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Tashigi_Cries_For_Smoker%27s_Encouragement.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Tashigi cries after receiving stimulus phrases from Smoker.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After the events of the <a href="/wiki/Arabasta_Arc" title="Arabasta Arc">Arabasta Arc</a>, Tashigi could not contain her frustration for needing the aid of the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a> in order to apprehend <a href="/wiki/Crocodile" title="Crocodile">Crocodile</a>, especially after Smoker praised her efforts through the whole ordeal. Smoker thought Tashigi was brave for being able to acknowledge her own weakness, urging his other subordinates to follow her example. It is worth noting that Tashigi's powerlessness regarding her encounter with Crocodile was one of the reasons Smoker declined the promotions and awards meant for them for the Warlord's capture (something they had little involvement in), as Smoker felt this was an insult to her honor.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Tashigi usually refers to her superior as "Smoker-san" (a simple Japanese honorific) as opposed to by his rank that other soldiers call him (i.e., "Vice Admiral Smoker"). Tashigi always follows Smoker's directives, rarely questioning them. However, during the events of the <a href="/wiki/Punk_Hazard_Arc" title="Punk Hazard Arc">Punk Hazard Arc</a>, Tashigi demonstrated some defiance towards her superior when she begged for her life in spite of Smoker's protests, berating the vice-admiral for being too prideful in a situation where the lives of his subordinates and the innocent children <a href="/wiki/Caesar_Clown" title="Caesar Clown">Caesar Clown</a> had captured for his experiments were in massive danger.<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Hina">Hina</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSmoker%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D11&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 200px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/11/Smoker_and_Hina_in_Arabasta.png/revision/latest?cb=20230316020307" class="image"><img alt="Smoker and Hina in Arabasta" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="150" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Smoker and Hina in Arabasta.png" data-image-key="Smoker_and_Hina_in_Arabasta.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/11/Smoker_and_Hina_in_Arabasta.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230316020307" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/11/Smoker_and_Hina_in_Arabasta.png/revision/latest?cb=20230316020307" class="image"><img alt="Smoker and Hina in Arabasta" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/11/Smoker_and_Hina_in_Arabasta.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230316020307" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="150" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Smoker and Hina in Arabasta.png" data-image-key="Smoker_and_Hina_in_Arabasta.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/11/Smoker_and_Hina_in_Arabasta.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230316020307" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Smoker_and_Hina_in_Arabasta.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Smoker and Hina working together in a mission.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Smoker has close ties with <a href="/wiki/Hina" title="Hina">Hina</a>, as she is a personal friend from their days of training. She has stood up for Smoker in situations that could have gotten him fired, which were apparently numerous.<sup id="cite_ref-sbs27_6-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sbs27-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> This was further established in present time when Smoker talked back to the higher-ups who wanted to promote him, with Hina desperately reminding Smoker of the potential consequences for insubordination.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Because they have known each other for a long time, Hina calls him Smoker-kun (a Japanese honorific used usually for younger peers) while Smoker addresses Hina by her name alone (which, in Japanese, shows either a sign of disrespect or closeness). Hina already seems to be used to Smoker's signature obstinacy, arguing with him in a casual, somewhat vitriolic manner. She is also aware of Smoker's softer side, to which Smoker just told her to "mind her own business".<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup><br style="clear:both;" />
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Kuzan">Kuzan</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSmoker%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D12&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/48/Kuzan_Treats_Smoker.png/revision/latest?cb=20191212045635" class="image"><img alt="Kuzan Treats Smoker" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="129" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kuzan Treats Smoker.png" data-image-key="Kuzan_Treats_Smoker.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/48/Kuzan_Treats_Smoker.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20191212045635" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/48/Kuzan_Treats_Smoker.png/revision/latest?cb=20191212045635" class="image"><img alt="Kuzan Treats Smoker" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/48/Kuzan_Treats_Smoker.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20191212045635" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="129" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kuzan Treats Smoker.png" data-image-key="Kuzan_Treats_Smoker.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/48/Kuzan_Treats_Smoker.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20191212045635" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kuzan_Treats_Smoker.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kuzan treats Smoker after being defeated by Doflamingo.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Smoker seems to be on good terms with <a href="/wiki/Kuzan" title="Kuzan">Kuzan</a>, as he requested Aokiji to pass a message to Monkey D. Luffy at some point after the Arabasta Arc,<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> and later convinced the then Admiral to negotiate with <a href="/wiki/Sengoku" title="Sengoku">Sengoku</a> for a transfer to the more dangerous <a href="/wiki/G-5" title="G-5">G-5</a> station in the <a href="/wiki/New_World" title="New World">New World</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> Although both Sengoku and Aokiji resigned before either could grant Smoker his request, the new Fleet Admiral, Sakazuki, was benign enough to transfer Smoker there. 
</p><p>Even after his resignation, Kuzan saved Smoker from being killed by <a href="/wiki/Donquixote_Doflamingo" title="Donquixote Doflamingo">Donquixote Doflamingo</a> on the basis that they were still friends, all while comforting Smoker about certain negative rumors that were surrounding the former Admiral and ensuring that he had not changed his ways after leaving the Marines.<sup id="cite_ref-c698_24-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c698-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Issho">Issho</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSmoker%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D13&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b7/Smoker_Talks_to_Issho_About_the_Warlords_System.png/revision/latest?cb=20200701004650" class="image"><img alt="Smoker Talks to Issho About the Warlords System" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Smoker Talks to Issho About the Warlords System.png" data-image-key="Smoker_Talks_to_Issho_About_the_Warlords_System.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b7/Smoker_Talks_to_Issho_About_the_Warlords_System.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20200701004650" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b7/Smoker_Talks_to_Issho_About_the_Warlords_System.png/revision/latest?cb=20200701004650" class="image"><img alt="Smoker Talks to Issho About the Warlords System" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b7/Smoker_Talks_to_Issho_About_the_Warlords_System.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20200701004650" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Smoker Talks to Issho About the Warlords System.png" data-image-key="Smoker_Talks_to_Issho_About_the_Warlords_System.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b7/Smoker_Talks_to_Issho_About_the_Warlords_System.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20200701004650" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Smoker_Talks_to_Issho_About_the_Warlords_System.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Smoker talks to Issho about the problems with the Seven Warlords of the Sea system.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Smoker appears to have become well acquainted with <a href="/wiki/Issho" title="Issho">Fujitora</a>, as he, like Kuzan, believes the Seven Warlords of the Sea system should be dissolved. He later expressed both his shock and gratitude to have learned that Fujitora did not let the government cover up the ordeal in Dressrosa as they did in Arabasta to which Smoker was grateful for and even admitted that if he were in Fujitora's position, he would not be able to do what Fujitora did.<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup><br style="clear:both;" />
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="G-5">G-5</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSmoker%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D14&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 200px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/11/Smoker_Giving_Orders_to_the_G-5.png/revision/latest?cb=20191216030352" class="image"><img alt="Smoker Giving Orders to the G-5" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="241" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Smoker Giving Orders to the G-5.png" data-image-key="Smoker_Giving_Orders_to_the_G-5.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/11/Smoker_Giving_Orders_to_the_G-5.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20191216030352" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/11/Smoker_Giving_Orders_to_the_G-5.png/revision/latest?cb=20191216030352" class="image"><img alt="Smoker Giving Orders to the G-5" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/11/Smoker_Giving_Orders_to_the_G-5.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20191216030352" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="241" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Smoker Giving Orders to the G-5.png" data-image-key="Smoker_Giving_Orders_to_the_G-5.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/11/Smoker_Giving_Orders_to_the_G-5.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20191216030352" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Smoker_Giving_Orders_to_the_G-5.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Smoker giving orders to the G-5.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Currently, as the base commander&#160;in charge of G-5, Smoker has authority over the personnel stationed there. The soldiers are known to be sadistic, prone to torturing, and ignoring regulations, but obey Smoker with no problem. Smoker, in turn, shows contempt for them due to their blatant disregard for laws.<sup id="cite_ref-reintro_2-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-reintro-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> Still, Smoker is protective of his troops, ordering Tashigi to make sure they are kept safe when he is not around, and the G-5 soldiers, likewise, care for Smoker's well-being, relying on him for leadership.<sup id="cite_ref-c670_26-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c670-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> When Smoker learned that Vergo had attacked their subordinates, he told his former superior he had no right to even lay a finger on his men.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Enemies">Enemies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSmoker%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D15&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Monkey_D._Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSmoker%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D16&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Smoker has a strong desire (or even an obsession) to arrest <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Luffy</a> dating back to when the pirate was about to be executed by <a href="/wiki/Buggy" title="Buggy">Buggy</a> in Loguetown. Smoker saw the smile Luffy gave off to mirror that of <a href="/wiki/Gol_D._Roger" title="Gol D. Roger">Gold Roger</a>'s twenty-two years ago and considered Luffy to be a potential danger to the world. Smoker has always wondered why Dragon would rescue Luffy in Loguetown, until Sengoku made it public that Dragon is Luffy's father, which intensified Smoker's thought about Luffy's dangerous potential.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/69/Smoker_Facing_Luffy_in_Marineford.png/revision/latest?cb=20230316021852" class="image"><img alt="Smoker Facing Luffy in Marineford" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Smoker Facing Luffy in Marineford.png" data-image-key="Smoker_Facing_Luffy_in_Marineford.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/69/Smoker_Facing_Luffy_in_Marineford.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230316021852" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/69/Smoker_Facing_Luffy_in_Marineford.png/revision/latest?cb=20230316021852" class="image"><img alt="Smoker Facing Luffy in Marineford" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/69/Smoker_Facing_Luffy_in_Marineford.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230316021852" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Smoker Facing Luffy in Marineford.png" data-image-key="Smoker_Facing_Luffy_in_Marineford.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/69/Smoker_Facing_Luffy_in_Marineford.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230316021852" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Smoker_Facing_Luffy_in_Marineford.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Smoker facing Luffy in Marineford.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ever since witnessing Luffy's smile during his aborted execution, Smoker has been relentless in trying to pursue Luffy and arrest him. Despite Luffy ordering Zoro to save Smoker from drowning after escaping the Rainbase Casino, Smoker still had the ambition to someday capture Luffy, only recouping him by letting him go that one time. Smoker is even willing to go as far as to the <a href="/wiki/New_World" title="New World">New World</a> to capture Luffy, and has waited two years for Luffy to finally arrive. Smoker is Luffy's longest running Marine adversary to date.
</p><p>Due to Smoker's desire to apprehend Luffy for such an extended period, he seems to have learned of Luffy's habits based on the various encounters with him as well as information from news reports. Smoker was able to correctly predict Luffy's desire to go to <a href="/wiki/Raijin_Island" title="Raijin Island">Raijin Island</a> due to the <a href="/wiki/Log_Pose#New_World_Log_Pose" title="Log Pose">Log Pose</a> pointing at the island being the most turbulent, fitting Luffy's reckless nature.<sup id="cite_ref-reintro_2-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-reintro-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> Indeed, Luffy was originally planning to go there,<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> were he not diverted by a distress call from <a href="/wiki/Punk_Hazard" title="Punk Hazard">Punk Hazard</a>. Smoker was also willing to enter Punk Hazard to pursue Luffy, despite the Government placing the island off-limits. When he finally saw Luffy for the first time in two years, he immediately attacked him despite Smoker being stuck in Tashigi’s body due to Law’s abilities. He was also very embarrassed when Luffy laughed at him because of his peculiar situation and became infuriated when Luffy refused to battle him in that condition.<sup id="cite_ref-c670_26-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c670-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> Due to the situation, when <a href="/wiki/Trafalgar_D._Water_Law" title="Trafalgar D. Water Law">Trafalgar Law</a> and Luffy allied with each other and defeated <a href="/wiki/Caesar_Clown" title="Caesar Clown">Caesar Clown</a>, Smoker once again let Luffy go.
</p><p>However, Smoker's desire to arrest him is more out of a sense of duty as a Marine and caution due to being aware of the threat that Luffy may pose to the World Government in the future, as Smoker is not shown to have any particular or specific hatred towards him. In the same way, Luffy himself does not appear to hate Smoker. In fact, he even admitted that he liked the Marine, much to Smoker's annoyance. During the <a href="/wiki/Arabasta_Arc" title="Arabasta Arc">Arabasta Arc</a>, the Straw Hat captain ordered <a href="/wiki/Roronoa_Zoro" title="Roronoa Zoro">Roronoa Zoro</a> to save him when they were escaping the flooded <a href="/wiki/Rain_Dinners" title="Rain Dinners">Rain Dinners</a> secret chamber, solely because he did not want the Marine to drown (knowing that Devil Fruit users are helpless underwater). Still, Luffy used to be rather afraid of Smoker due to having no reliable way to counter his Logia abilities, leading to several pursuits where Luffy desperately attempted to shake off Smoker and his forces.
</p><p>After learning <a href="/wiki/Haki" title="Haki">Haki</a>, Luffy does not seem to fear Smoker anymore, having proclaimed his desire to have a rematch with the Marine vice-admiral someday, postponing it due to Smoker's "<a href="/wiki/Ope_Ope_no_Mi" title="Ope Ope no Mi">handicap</a>" at the time. He also appears to view Smoker as more of a friend than an enemy now, even showing concern for his well-being after witnessing his unconscious body laying around right after the Marine's fight with Trafalgar Law.<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Portgas_D._Ace">Portgas D. Ace</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSmoker%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D17&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Smoker made an enemy of <a href="/wiki/Portgas_D._Ace" title="Portgas D. Ace">Ace</a> during the <a href="/wiki/Arabasta_Arc" title="Arabasta Arc">Arabasta Arc</a>. Smoker simply stated that he could not let a pirate such as Ace go so easily, but when Luffy showed up, the Marine captain started prioritizing the Straw Hat captain while ignoring the Whitebeard pirate. 
</p><p>Smoker clashed with Ace when the latter stood in his way in order to protect Luffy, with Smoker cursing Luffy's brother for interfering on his chase.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Monkey_D._Dragon">Monkey D. Dragon</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSmoker%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D18&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Smoker only met the <a href="/wiki/Revolutionary_Army" title="Revolutionary Army">Revolutionary Army</a> leader, <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Dragon" title="Monkey D. Dragon">Monkey D. Dragon</a>, once, during the <a href="/wiki/Loguetown_Arc" title="Loguetown Arc">Loguetown Arc</a>. However, the revolutionary's sudden appearance left a lasting impression on Smoker's mind, since the Marine could not fathom why someone like Dragon would assist Luffy in escaping his clutches, which contributed to Smoker's desire to venture into the <a href="/wiki/Grand_Line" title="Grand Line">Grand Line</a> after the Straw Hat Pirates. 
</p><p>Smoker would eventually learn about the connection between Dragon and Luffy during the <a href="/wiki/Summit_War_of_Marineford" title="Summit War of Marineford">Summit War of Marineford</a>, finally getting an answer to the events of that day.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea">Seven Warlords of the Sea</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSmoker%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D19&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Smoker is known to hate the <a href="/wiki/Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea" title="Seven Warlords of the Sea">Seven Warlords of the Sea</a>, viewing them as nothing more than pirates, and thus not worth trusting. Smoker involved himself in Warlord-related schemes at least twice and has confronted several of them either because he meddled into their affairs or attacked someone they cared about.
</p><p>Smoker indirectly contributed to the dissolution of the Warlord system when he told Admiral Fujitora about the <a href="/wiki/Arabasta_Arc" title="Arabasta Arc">Arabasta incident</a>, inspiring the admiral to elaborate a plan of his own to let the world witness the chaos the Warlords were creating.
</p><p>After the Warlord system was disbanded, Smoker is once more enemies with the remaining of the former Warlords.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Crocodile">Crocodile</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSmoker%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D20&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><a href="/wiki/Crocodile" title="Crocodile">Crocodile</a> imprisoned Smoker along with the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a> in a <a href="/wiki/Seastone" title="Seastone">Seastone</a> Cage at <a href="/wiki/Rain_Dinners" title="Rain Dinners">Rain Dinners</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> The Baroque Works leader planned to silence the marine captain by killing him alongside the Straw Hats while covering up his death. Later on, Crocodile stumbled into a badly wounded Tashigi and mocked the fact Smoker was not around to help her, thinking he had fled Arabasta.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>During the Summit War of Marineford, Smoker was very surprised to see Luffy cooperating with Crocodile.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Boa_Hancock">Boa Hancock</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSmoker%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D21&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 200px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c7/Hancock_Protects_Luffy_from_Smoker.png/revision/latest?cb=20220910140202" class="image"><img alt="Hancock Protects Luffy from Smoker" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="113" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hancock Protects Luffy from Smoker.png" data-image-key="Hancock_Protects_Luffy_from_Smoker.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c7/Hancock_Protects_Luffy_from_Smoker.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20220910140202" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c7/Hancock_Protects_Luffy_from_Smoker.png/revision/latest?cb=20220910140202" class="image"><img alt="Hancock Protects Luffy from Smoker" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c7/Hancock_Protects_Luffy_from_Smoker.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20220910140202" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="113" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hancock Protects Luffy from Smoker.png" data-image-key="Hancock_Protects_Luffy_from_Smoker.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c7/Hancock_Protects_Luffy_from_Smoker.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20220910140202" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hancock_Protects_Luffy_from_Smoker.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hancock protects Luffy from Smoker.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p><a href="/wiki/Boa_Hancock" title="Boa Hancock">Hancock</a> considers Smoker a personal enemy after he pinned down and attempted to kill Luffy. Hancock swore to "rip him to shreds and feed him to beasts".<sup id="cite_ref-c559_33-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c559-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> Hancock intercepted Smoker when he tried to attack Luffy once more, breaking his jitte in the process. Smoker warned Hancock that her actions might lead to her <a href="/wiki/Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea" title="Seven Warlords of the Sea">Warlord of the Sea</a> status being revoked, something that Hancock was convinced would not happen due to her beauty.<sup id="cite_ref-c560_34-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c560-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Donquixote_Doflamingo">Donquixote Doflamingo</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSmoker%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D22&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 200px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/37/Smoker_and_Doflamingo_Face_to_Face.png/revision/latest?cb=20230731225538" class="image"><img alt="Smoker and Doflamingo Face to Face" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="113" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Smoker and Doflamingo Face to Face.png" data-image-key="Smoker_and_Doflamingo_Face_to_Face.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/37/Smoker_and_Doflamingo_Face_to_Face.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230731225538" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/37/Smoker_and_Doflamingo_Face_to_Face.png/revision/latest?cb=20230731225538" class="image"><img alt="Smoker and Doflamingo Face to Face" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/37/Smoker_and_Doflamingo_Face_to_Face.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230731225538" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="113" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Smoker and Doflamingo Face to Face.png" data-image-key="Smoker_and_Doflamingo_Face_to_Face.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/37/Smoker_and_Doflamingo_Face_to_Face.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230731225538" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Smoker_and_Doflamingo_Face_to_Face.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Smoker and Doflamingo face to face in Punk Hazard.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When <a href="/wiki/Donquixote_Doflamingo" title="Donquixote Doflamingo">Donquixote Doflamingo</a> arrived at <a href="/wiki/Punk_Hazard" title="Punk Hazard">Punk Hazard</a> looking for Law and the Straw Hats after <a href="/wiki/Punk_Hazard_Arc" title="Punk Hazard Arc">the events that had transpired there</a>, he began attacking the G-5 Marines that were still doing rescue work in the island. Doflamingo demanded Smoker to reveal the whereabouts of the newly formed <a href="/wiki/Pirate_Alliance" title="Pirate Alliance">Pirate Alliance</a>, to which Smoker refused while derisively bringing up Vergo's involvement in the whole episode. Figuring that Smoker had learned a lot about his <a href="/wiki/Underworld" title="Underworld">underworld</a> operations, Doflamingo was left with no choice but to try silencing the vice-admiral. 
</p><p>After the intervention of <a href="/wiki/Kuzan" title="Kuzan">Kuzan</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-c698_24-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c698-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> Doflamingo spared Smoker's life as he did not want to risk fighting a former Admiral.<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Trafalgar_D._Water_Law">Trafalgar D. Water Law</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSmoker%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D23&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 200px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/87/Smoker_and_Law_Cooperating.png/revision/latest?cb=20200701004703" class="image"><img alt="Smoker and Law Cooperating" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="154" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Smoker and Law Cooperating.png" data-image-key="Smoker_and_Law_Cooperating.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/87/Smoker_and_Law_Cooperating.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20200701004703" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/87/Smoker_and_Law_Cooperating.png/revision/latest?cb=20200701004703" class="image"><img alt="Smoker and Law Cooperating" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/87/Smoker_and_Law_Cooperating.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20200701004703" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="154" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Smoker and Law Cooperating.png" data-image-key="Smoker_and_Law_Cooperating.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/87/Smoker_and_Law_Cooperating.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20200701004703" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Smoker_and_Law_Cooperating.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Smoker cooperates with Trafalgar Law to flee Caesar's laboratory.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When Smoker encountered <a href="/wiki/Trafalgar_D._Water_Law" title="Trafalgar D. Water Law">Trafalgar Law</a> at <a href="/wiki/Punk_Hazard" title="Punk Hazard">Punk Hazard</a>, he demanded answers from the then Warlord of the Sea about the mysteries surrounding the island, some regarding who Law was working for, indicating a hidden agenda.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> They battled each other, and Law managed to gain the upper hand by stealing Smoker's heart with his <a href="/wiki/Ope_Ope_no_Mi" title="Ope Ope no Mi">Mes</a> attack. While Smoker yielded in defeat, Law commented that he did not have to tell him anything,<sup id="cite_ref-Smoker_vs._Law_37-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Smoker_vs._Law-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> switching Smoker and Tashigi's bodies so they would be unable to get in his way again.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>However, once Law, Luffy, Smoker and Tashigi all got captured by Caesar Clown, they formed a temporary alliance in order to defeat the evil scientist and his ally Vergo. Smoker was reluctant about joining forces with Law due to the conditions he had set for him to change back his and Tashigi's bodies (which was to not mention his or Luffy's involvement in subsequent reports), but was convinced by a desperate Tashigi to accept his terms for the sake of his men. Law also reaffirmed that Smoker was under his debt since he could have just killed him instead.<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Later on, in the SAD Production Room, Smoker inadvertently saved Law by taking over his fight with Vergo, managing to swipe back Law's heart from Vergo's possession and thus getting even with the Warlord. With Vergo having been dealt with, Law and Smoker worked together to find a means of escaping the island for the others to use. Afterwards, while everybody else partied over Caesar's defeat, Smoker had a small chat with Law and showed curiosity about what kind of plan he had in mind while allying with the Straw Hats. Law left Smoker with only a <a href="/wiki/Green_Bit" title="Green Bit">small cryptic clue</a> about his next steps, which Smoker seemingly noted in his mission report to <a href="/wiki/New_Marineford" title="New Marineford">New Marineford</a>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Caesar_Clown">Caesar Clown</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSmoker%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D24&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Caesar viewed Smoker as a threat to his operations at Punk Hazard. Describing the vice-admiral as a "pain-in-the-neck", Caesar was seemingly aware of Smoker's reputation as a stubborn and meddlesome marine.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> When Law stole Smoker's heart and handed it to Caesar as a gift, Caesar became pleased.
</p><p>After being defeated by Luffy, Caesar attempted to take Smoker down with him as revenge, unaware that the heart Law had given to him was in fact <a href="/wiki/Monet" title="Monet">Monet</a>'s.<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Vergo">Vergo</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSmoker%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D25&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>When he was still base commander, <a href="/wiki/Vergo" title="Vergo">Vergo</a> put on a friendly front to soldiers and civilians in order to avoid suspicion. He admitted that he had been concerned about Smoker's transfer to G-5, mentioning that he had to put up the largest possible guard to prevent the newly transferred Marine from finding out his true affiliation. Vergo also expressed the desire to murder both Smoker and Tashigi "by accident", since they now knew about his secret identity.<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> After being released from his confinement, Smoker expressed disdain for his colleague's felonies and intended to battle him alone in retribution for his treason against the <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">Marines</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Non-Canon_2">Non-Canon</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSmoker%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D26&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Daddy_Masterson">Daddy Masterson</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSmoker%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D27&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><a href="/wiki/Daddy_Masterson" title="Daddy Masterson">Daddy</a> is apparently very close to Smoker, with the latter being familiar enough with Daddy's daughter <a href="/wiki/Carol" title="Carol">Carol</a> (Daddy refers to Smoker as "Uncle Smoker" to Carol). Daddy often hands over the pirates he catches for Smoker to imprison. Smoker claims that it is unfortunate that the Marines' best sniper was reduced to a common bounty hunter, demonstrating his respect for Daddy's skills.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Abilities_and_Powers">Abilities and Powers</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSmoker%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D28&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Smoker is a formidable combatant, as on top of his sheer strength, his <a href="/wiki/Logia" title="Logia">Logia</a> <a href="/wiki/Moku_Moku_no_Mi" title="Moku Moku no Mi">Devil Fruit</a> abilities set him apart from most Marines of his rank. Before Luffy came, it was said that pirate activity in Loguetown had dropped down significantly since Smoker's arrival, a testament to his competency. In <a href="/wiki/Loguetown" title="Loguetown">Loguetown</a>, he was on the verge of arresting Luffy during their first encounter, and would have succeeded had it not been for Luffy's father, <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Dragon" title="Monkey D. Dragon">Monkey D. Dragon</a>, interfering.<sup id="cite_ref-c100_45-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c100-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup> As a result, Luffy resorted to running away from Smoker every time he spotted him due to not yet knowing how to use <a href="/wiki/Haki/Armament_Haki" title="Haki/Armament Haki">Armament Haki</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After the <a href="/wiki/Enies_Lobby" title="Enies Lobby">Enies Lobby</a> events, Smoker was shown unsatisfied in capturing a pirate with a bounty of <span style="white-space:nowrap;"><a href="/wiki/Belly" title="Belly"><img alt="Beli" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="12" height="20" data-image-name="Beli.png" data-image-key="Beli.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/de/Beli.png/revision/latest?cb=20141206091723" class="lazyload" /></a></span>50,000,000 and already considered moving to the <a href="/wiki/New_World" title="New World">New World</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-post-Enies_Lobby_arc_4-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-post-Enies_Lobby_arc-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> During the <a href="/wiki/Summit_War_of_Marineford" title="Summit War of Marineford">Summit War of Marineford</a>, he again defeated Luffy, who was already a <a href="/wiki/Super_Rookie" title="Super Rookie">supernova</a>, effortlessly and could have captured him, if <a href="/wiki/Boa_Hancock" title="Boa Hancock">Hancock</a> had not interfered.
</p><p>By the end of the Summit War of Marineford, Smoker's overall strength had granted him enough confidence to request a transfer to the <a href="/wiki/G-5" title="G-5">G-5</a> Marine Branch in the New World. It was said that the soldiers of this branch were insane, cruel, and merciless, regularly torturing pirates through various methods. They were known for not following orders, but Smoker, who is very much similar, managed to earn their loyalty and obedience, to the point of worship.<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> With <a href="/wiki/Vergo" title="Vergo">Vergo</a>'s treason and death, Smoker took over as base commander, effectively becoming the highest authority within the branch.
</p><p>Smoker's skills in pursuing and ensnaring enemies are regarded as top-notch, being the source of his "White Hunter" moniker. Luffy being the first person to ever escape his clutches is what causes him to fearlessly tackle more dangerous seas.
</p><p>After the timeskip, Smoker and his crew managed to capture several pirates who were liberated from <a href="/wiki/Hody_Jones" title="Hody Jones">Hody</a>'s control at once.<sup id="cite_ref-c652_48-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c652-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> During his time on <a href="/wiki/Punk_Hazard" title="Punk Hazard">Punk Hazard</a>, he managed to give <a href="/wiki/Trafalgar_D._Water_Law" title="Trafalgar D. Water Law">Trafalgar Law</a>, a Warlord of the Sea and part of the <a href="/wiki/Worst_Generation" title="Worst Generation">Worst Generation</a>, a hard time in combat before he was ultimately defeated.<sup id="cite_ref-Smoker_vs._Law_37-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Smoker_vs._Law-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> He also fought fellow his fellow vice admiral, <a href="/wiki/Vergo" title="Vergo">Vergo</a>, who is also one of the strongest members of the <a href="/wiki/Donquixote_Pirates" title="Donquixote Pirates">Donquixote Pirates</a>, on relatively equal terms, despite Vergo's superior mastery of Haki, although in the end he was defeated.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Even after having his mind switched to <a href="/wiki/Tashigi" title="Tashigi">Tashigi</a>'s body, Smoker managed to strike Luffy, surprising the Straw Hat captain, who wondered how "Tashigi" had gotten so strong since two years ago. Also, despite not being in his original body, Smoker easily defeated some of <a href="/wiki/Caesar_Clown" title="Caesar Clown">Caesar</a>’s subordinates through his normal skills alone.<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Smoker has both excellent hearing and memory, best shown during the <a href="/wiki/Arabasta_Arc" title="Arabasta Arc">Arabasta Arc</a>, where he was able to identify a certain <a href="/wiki/Animal_Species/Arabasta_Saga#Bananawani" title="Animal Species/Arabasta Saga">Bananawani</a> from a whole pack solely by memorizing its growl. While he may not look like it, Smoker is a clever and intelligent interrogator, easily tricking <a href="/wiki/Mr._11" title="Mr. 11">Mr. 11</a> into revealing his affiliation to <a href="/wiki/Baroque_Works" title="Baroque Works">Baroque Works</a> through deceit. Being highly observant, Smoker was the only one who noticed the unusual icebergs that blocked their path during their trip to Punk Hazard, and was suspicious of the ever present gas that lingers around the island, both of which were being manipulated by the enemy. As a leader and strategist, Smoker is extremely efficient at his job, mobilizing his forces in a clear and concise manner during times of crisis.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Physical_Abilities">Physical Abilities</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSmoker%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D29&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>As evident by his strong build, Smoker possesses incredible physical strength. During his confrontation with Luffy in Loguetown, he was able to jump about two stories high without difficulty while holding the pirate and pin him down so that unable to retaliate, a noteworthy feat considering Luffy's superhuman physical power.<sup id="cite_ref-c100_45-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c100-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup> 
</p><p>He also has vast durability and resistance. Smoker was able to stand back up with no visible damage and without effort after receiving a Haki-enhanced kick from Boa Hancock, whose attacks were strong enough to shatter stone and <a href="/wiki/Pacifista" title="Pacifista">Pacifista</a> armor (though Hancock's kick was primarily to get him off of Luffy).
</p><p>After the timeskip, Smoker's physical strength has become significantly more powerful, being able to grab Law's neck with one hand, slice through a rock twice his size with a single blow, and elbow blood out of his partner, Vergo. His stamina and durability also improved as he can take a lot of Vergo's Haki-enhanced hits and keep fighting.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Devil_Fruit">Devil Fruit</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSmoker%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D30&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl><dd><i>Further information: <a href="/wiki/Moku_Moku_no_Mi" title="Moku Moku no Mi">Moku Moku no Mi</a></i></dd></dl>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/64/Logia_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20220328100112" class="image"><img alt="Logia Infobox" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Logia Infobox.png" data-image-key="Logia_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/64/Logia_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220328100112" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/64/Logia_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20220328100112" class="image"><img alt="Logia Infobox" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/64/Logia_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220328100112" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Logia Infobox.png" data-image-key="Logia_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/64/Logia_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220328100112" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Logia_Infobox.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Smoker uses the Moku Moku no Mi.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Smoker ate the Moku Moku no Mi, a <a href="/wiki/Logia" title="Logia">Logia</a>-type <a href="/wiki/Devil_Fruit" title="Devil Fruit">Devil Fruit</a> that allows him to create, control and transform his body into smoke. He can manipulate the smoke's density, even to the point of solidifying it, allowing him to hold and constrict others within it. Like most Logia users, he can fly by turning his lower body into smoke and propelling himself like a rocket.
</p><p>He can use his smoke to surround his opponents to trap and/or bind them. Due to smoke being a gas, it has high maneuverability and irregular movements, allowing him to easily cover the battlefield in smoke as his opponents pointlessly try to escape it. Once his smoke is surrounding his enemies, he can increase its density, turning it solid and restraining his victims.
</p><p>He can also use his smoke as a blunt weapon. He can shoot powerful jets of smoke at his opponents to strike them with great force.
</p><p>Using his smoke powers, Smoker can power up the engines of his motorbike, the <a href="/wiki/Billower_Bike" title="Billower Bike">Billower Bike</a>, for ground transportation.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Weapons">Weapons</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSmoker%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D31&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Nanashaku_Jitte">Nanashaku Jitte</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSmoker%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D32&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<dl><dd><i>Further information: <a href="/wiki/Nanashaku_Jitte" title="Nanashaku Jitte">Nanashaku Jitte</a></i></dd></dl>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 160px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/01/Nanashaku_Jitte_in_Smoker%27s_Back.png/revision/latest?cb=20240314113701" class="image"><img alt="Nanashaku Jitte in Smoker&#39;s Back" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="160" height="215" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Nanashaku Jitte in Smoker&#39;s Back.png" data-image-key="Nanashaku_Jitte_in_Smoker%27s_Back.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/01/Nanashaku_Jitte_in_Smoker%27s_Back.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/160?cb=20240314113701" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/01/Nanashaku_Jitte_in_Smoker%27s_Back.png/revision/latest?cb=20240314113701" class="image"><img alt="Nanashaku Jitte in Smoker&#39;s Back" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/01/Nanashaku_Jitte_in_Smoker%27s_Back.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/160?cb=20240314113701" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="160" height="215" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Nanashaku Jitte in Smoker&#39;s Back.png" data-image-key="Nanashaku_Jitte_in_Smoker%27s_Back.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/01/Nanashaku_Jitte_in_Smoker%27s_Back.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/160?cb=20240314113701" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Nanashaku_Jitte_in_Smoker%27s_Back.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Smoker's jitte strapped to his back.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Smoker's main weapon is a large <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/jitte" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:jitte">jitte</a> that is tipped with <a href="/wiki/Seastone" title="Seastone">Seastone</a>, a material that affects Devil Fruit users in a similar way to the sea, which he uses to subdue criminal Devil Fruit users.
</p><p>Since only the tip is Seastone, it does not affect Smoker himself. He keeps the tip hanging in the air at all times, and his thick clothing provides further protection. When he turns into smoke, the weapon does not turn into smoke with him because of the Seastone. Instead, he carries it with him while in smoke form.
</p><p>Smoker seems to be very proficient in wielding the jitte, taking enemies by surprise and using the weapon to deliver strong blunt attacks. The jitte was broken in half when Boa Hancock kicked it, which led it to crumble. After the timeskip, the jitte has shown to have been repaired. Its hilt is white in the manga, but red in the anime. Also, in the manga and its related merchandise and products, it seems to be much longer than in the anime, almost reaching down to Smoker's feet.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Billower_Bike">Billower Bike</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSmoker%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D33&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<dl><dd><i>Further information: <a href="/wiki/Billower_Bike" title="Billower Bike">Billower Bike</a></i></dd></dl>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 200px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/5d/Billower_Bike_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20240616200004" class="image"><img alt="Billower Bike Infobox" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Billower Bike Infobox.png" data-image-key="Billower_Bike_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/5d/Billower_Bike_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20240616200004" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/5d/Billower_Bike_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20240616200004" class="image"><img alt="Billower Bike Infobox" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/5d/Billower_Bike_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20240616200004" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Billower Bike Infobox.png" data-image-key="Billower_Bike_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/5d/Billower_Bike_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20240616200004" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Billower_Bike_Infobox.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Smoker driving the Billower Bike.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The Billower Bike is used for ground transportation. It is a wide bike with three wheels (two large ones at the rear, and a smaller one in front) and its engines are powered by his <a href="/wiki/Moku_Moku_no_Mi" title="Moku Moku no Mi">Moku Moku no Mi</a> powers. Additionally, Smoker can traverse water with the bike.<br style="clear:both;" />
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Haki">Haki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSmoker%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D34&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/Haki" title="Haki">Haki</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f4/White_Blow.png/revision/latest?cb=20240307140409" class="image"><img alt="White Blow" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="White Blow.png" data-image-key="White_Blow.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f4/White_Blow.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240307140409" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f4/White_Blow.png/revision/latest?cb=20240307140409" class="image"><img alt="White Blow" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f4/White_Blow.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240307140409" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="White Blow.png" data-image-key="White_Blow.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f4/White_Blow.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240307140409" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:White_Blow.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Smoker using Armament Haki to empower a punch.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Before the timeskip, Smoker was not able to use Haki, although he had some knowledge of it. This put him at a disadvantage against the Warlord of the Sea Boa Hancock, who had mastery of the ability and could counter his Logia nature.<sup id="cite_ref-Knowledge_51-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Knowledge-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>During the timeskip, Smoker was promoted to vice admiral, confirming that he can use the ability.<sup id="cite_ref-vicehaki_52-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vicehaki-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Armament_Haki">Armament Haki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSmoker%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D35&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Smoker possesses the ability to use <a href="/wiki/Haki/Armament_Haki" title="Haki/Armament Haki">Armament Haki</a>. During his battle with <a href="/wiki/Vergo" title="Vergo">Vergo</a>, he landed a punch where his hand and part of his arm were completely black, demonstrating the use of Hardening.<sup id="cite_ref-Fist_53-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Fist-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> He later did the same with his elbow when striking Vergo in the face.<sup id="cite_ref-Elbow_54-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Elbow-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup> He can also imbue his Nanashaku Jitte with Haki, enhancing the strength of its strikes.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Observation_Haki">Observation Haki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSmoker%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D36&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Smoker possesses the ability to use <a href="/wiki/Haki/Observation_Haki" title="Haki/Observation Haki">Observation Haki</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_5-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> as he sensed that <a href="/wiki/Tashigi" title="Tashigi">Tashigi</a>'s Haki was not strong enough to counter <a href="/wiki/Trafalgar_D._Water_Law" title="Trafalgar D. Water Law">Law</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Ope_Ope_no_Mi" title="Ope Ope no Mi">ability</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
