<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Anime_and_Manga_Differences">Anime and Manga Differences</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSmoker%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D39&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Appearance_2">Appearance</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSmoker%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D40&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In the manga, his hair color is pure white; the anime initially tinted it a greenish-grey color, but changed to match the manga from the <a href="/wiki/Punk_Hazard_Arc" title="Punk Hazard Arc">Punk Hazard Arc</a> on. His jacket's fur trim also differs between mediums, with the manga portraying it as a bluish color and the anime a deep green; in this case, the manga eventually changed its color scheme to follow the anime.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-e48_11-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-e48-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div style="text-align: center; font-size: 0.7em; color: ; margin: 0.7em 0;"><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 157px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 157px; height: 157px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/20/Smoker_Pre_Timeskip_Portrait.png/revision/latest?cb=20200105084734" class="image"><img alt="Smoker Pre Timeskip Portrait" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="135" height="135" data-image-name="Smoker Pre Timeskip Portrait.png" data-image-key="Smoker_Pre_Timeskip_Portrait.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/20/Smoker_Pre_Timeskip_Portrait.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/135?cb=20200105084734" class="lazyload" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Smoker's white hair in the manga.
</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 157px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 157px; height: 157px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/60/Smoker_Greenish-Grey_Hair_Portrait.png/revision/latest?cb=20200626181151" class="image"><img alt="Smoker Greenish-Grey Hair Portrait" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="135" height="135" data-image-name="Smoker Greenish-Grey Hair Portrait.png" data-image-key="Smoker_Greenish-Grey_Hair_Portrait.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/60/Smoker_Greenish-Grey_Hair_Portrait.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/135?cb=20200626181151" class="lazyload" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Smoker's greenish-grey hair in the anime.
</div></span></div>
<p>Additionally, his cigar-bands are labeled "MARINE" in the manga, implying they come from a specialty supplier. This, like most of the manga's small-print details, is omitted from the anime.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Loguetown_Arc">Loguetown Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSmoker%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D41&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 220px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d3/Smoker_During_Gold_Roger%27s_Execution.png/revision/latest?cb=20200129143001" class="image"><img alt="Smoker During Gold Roger&#39;s Execution" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="220" height="124" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Smoker During Gold Roger&#39;s Execution.png" data-image-key="Smoker_During_Gold_Roger%27s_Execution.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d3/Smoker_During_Gold_Roger%27s_Execution.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20200129143001" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d3/Smoker_During_Gold_Roger%27s_Execution.png/revision/latest?cb=20200129143001" class="image"><img alt="Smoker During Gold Roger&#39;s Execution" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d3/Smoker_During_Gold_Roger%27s_Execution.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20200129143001" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="220" height="124" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Smoker During Gold Roger&#39;s Execution.png" data-image-key="Smoker_During_Gold_Roger%27s_Execution.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d3/Smoker_During_Gold_Roger%27s_Execution.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20200129143001" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Smoker_During_Gold_Roger%27s_Execution.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Young Smoker witnesses <a href="/wiki/Gol_D._Roger" title="Gol D. Roger">Gold Roger</a>'s execution, as seen in the anime.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In the anime, the subplot on Smoker's backstory he mentions about Gold Roger is expanded on in Loguetown, showing that he was at Roger's execution when he was a child.<sup id="cite_ref-e48_11-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-e48-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> However, in the manga, Smoker's comments on Roger were merely just a passing comment and only Roger's face is seen.<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Instead of learning about Luffy when he was about to be executed by Buggy and Alvida,<sup id="cite_ref-intro_3-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-intro-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> Smoker learns about him earlier. He is informed that some pirates are creating havoc in the harbor. Thinking that this crew is the Straw Hat Pirates, Smoker goes to investigate. There he finds an elderly pirate called <a href="/wiki/Gally" title="Gally">Crescent Moon Gally</a> who has a bounty of 3,450,000. He and his crew are seen raiding buildings at Loguetown before being captured, however he is notably disappointed when he finds out that Gally was not the man he was looking for. Luffy then appears and asks Smoker where the execution gallows are. Using his smoke, he guides Luffy to the gallows without having any idea who he was. It wasn't until he was in <a href="/wiki/Raoul" title="Raoul">Raoul</a>'s bar that he figured out who the boy he helped was. He raced through town to the gallows to intercept and challenge him. Even without using his Devil Fruit powers, Smoker manages to gain the upper hand against Luffy, who then manages to accidentally send himself flying into another part of town.<sup id="cite_ref-e48_11-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-e48-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Later, <a href="/wiki/Daddy_Masterson" title="Daddy Masterson">Daddy Masterson</a> is seen talking to then-Captain Smoker and asking him to sign a release. Smoker asks him about his daughter and claims it is sad how the Marines' best sniper is reduced to a common bounty hunter. Just as he is about to leave, Smoker tells him to say hi to Carol for him at which Daddy replies; "I'll tell her Uncle Smoker said hello." Immediately after he leaves the room Tashigi asks him if the man was Daddy Masterson and Smoker replies with great praise and from there he refers to him as an equal.<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup> In the anime during the race back to the Going Merry, Luffy fights Smoker alone and the Marines attack the ship forcing Nami to pull the Going Merry away from the docks. Sanji's role is placed here rather than the fight with Smoker as he fights the Marines attacking the ship.<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Jitte">Jitte</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSmoker%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D42&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>During <a href="/wiki/Episode_488" title="Episode 488">Episode 488</a>, Smoker was shown using his jitte, even though Hancock had destroyed it earlier.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Translation_and_Dub_Issues">Translation and Dub Issues</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSmoker%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D43&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Per its standard editing policies, the <a href="/wiki/4Kids_Entertainment" title="4Kids Entertainment">4Kids-dubbed anime</a> - in addition to renaming him <i>Chaser</i> - removes all of his cigars and the "justice"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">正義</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Seigi</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span> kanji on his jacket; however, it usually leaves the smoke-trails around his face unedited, excusing them as a side-effect of his abilities. Localizations of contemporary video games such as <a href="/wiki/One_Piece:_Grand_Battle!_Rush!" title="One Piece: Grand Battle! Rush!"><i>Grand Battle!</i></a> and <i><a href="/wiki/One_Piece:_Unlimited_Adventure" title="One Piece: Unlimited Adventure">Unlimited Adventure</a></i> typically leave his jacket unedited as well, removing only his in-use cigars.
</p><p>4Kids' adaptation of the <a href="/wiki/Loguetown_Arc" title="Loguetown Arc">Loguetown Arc</a> similarly censors his alcohol preferences, having him raid <a href="/wiki/Raoul" title="Raoul">Raoul</a>'s bar for "power juice" rather than rum.
</p><p>Finally, 4Kids' localization of <i><a href="/wiki/One_Piece:_Pirates_Carnival" title="One Piece: Pirates Carnival">Pirates Carnival</a></i> uses him to host a mini-game originally hosted by <a href="/wiki/Paulie" title="Paulie">Paulie</a> (as it had made no preparations for dubbing the <a href="/wiki/Water_7_Arc" title="Water 7 Arc">Water 7 Arc</a>), his smoke abilities substituting for Paulie's <a href="/wiki/Rope_Action" title="Rope Action">Rope Action</a>. The mini-game's overall setup - to <a href="/wiki/Chapter_326" title="Chapter 326">retrieve several suitcases</a> from a lumberyard - is unchanged, apart from the lumberyard's <a href="/wiki/Dock_1" title="Dock 1">Dock 1</a> label being painted over with a "NAVY" emblem.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Merchandise">Merchandise</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSmoker%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D44&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Smoker has been the choice character in many forms of merchandise. He has been featured in the series of models <a href="/wiki/Portrait_of_Pirates" title="Portrait of Pirates">Portrait of Pirates</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Video_Games_2">Video Games</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSmoker%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D45&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Other_Appearances">Other Appearances</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSmoker%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D50&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Other_Media">Other Media</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSmoker%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D51&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li>Smoker appears in <i><a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Premier_Show#One_Piece_Premier_Show_2012" title="One Piece Premier Show">One Piece Premier Show 2012</a></i> as one of <a href="/wiki/Chameleone" title="Chameleone">Chameleone</a>'s transformations.</li>
<li>In <i><a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Premier_Show#One_Piece_Premier_Show_2013" title="One Piece Premier Show">One Piece Premier Show 2013</a></i>, Smoker leads a group of Marines to investigate a number of kidnappings on <a href="/wiki/Paradise_Island" title="Paradise Island">Paradise Island</a>.</li>
<li>Smoker appears in the 2018, Segment 1 show of <i><a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Water_Battle" title="One Piece Water Battle">One Piece Water Battle</a></i>. He also appears in the 2013 <i><a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Pirate_Sweeping_Operation" title="One Piece Pirate Sweeping Operation">One Piece Pirate Sweeping Operation</a></i> show.</li>
<li>In the second version of <i><a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Live_Attraction:_Phantom" title="One Piece Live Attraction: Phantom">One Piece Live Attraction: Phantom</a></i>, <a href="/wiki/Buggy" title="Buggy">Buggy</a> forces <a href="/wiki/Ann" title="Ann">Ann</a> to create a <a href="/wiki/Bijo_Bijo_no_Mi" title="Bijo Bijo no Mi">mirage</a> of Smoker to capture the Straw Hat Pirates.</li>
<li>Smoker appears in <i><a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates_vs._Marines_vs._Seven_Warlords_Holographic_Battle_Theater" title="Straw Hat Pirates vs. Marines vs. Seven Warlords Holographic Battle Theater">Straw Hat Pirates vs. Marines vs. Seven Warlords Holographic Battle Theater</a></i>.</li>
<li>An image of Smoker appears in the first <i><a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Water_Spectacle" title="One Piece Water Spectacle">One Piece Water Spectacle</a></i> show.</li>
<li>Smoker appears in the Nami and Marineford versions of the "<a href="/wiki/Hungry_Days" title="Hungry Days">Hungry Days</a>" commercials.</li></ul>
<div style="text-align: center; font-size: 0.7em; color: ; margin: 0.7em 0;"><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 142px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 142px; height: 172px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/ad/Smoker_Premier_Show.png/revision/latest?cb=20130806055055" class="image"><img alt="Smoker Premier Show" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="107" height="150" data-image-name="Smoker Premier Show.png" data-image-key="Smoker_Premier_Show.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/ad/Smoker_Premier_Show.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/107?cb=20130806055055" class="lazyload" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Smoker in <i>Premier Show 2012</i>.

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Trivia">Trivia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSmoker%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D52&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>Smoker is the first Logia-type Devil Fruit user to be revealed.
<ul><li>Smoker is also the first Logia-type Devil Fruit user in the <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">Marines</a>.</li></ul></li>
<li>Smoker is the first major character to be recast in the anime, with his original voice actor <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ginz%C5%8D_Matsuo" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Ginzō Matsuo">Ginzō Matsuo</a> (who died on August 25, 2001 of an acute <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Subarachnoid_hemorrhage" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Subarachnoid hemorrhage">subarachnoid hemorrhage</a>, making this his final role) being succeeded by the anime's narrator <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mahito_Ohba" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Mahito Ohba">Mahito Ohba</a> from <a href="/wiki/Episode_94" title="Episode 94">episode 94</a> on.</li>
<li>Smoker has cornered <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Luffy</a> on three occasions before the timeskip, and each time, he is saved by a relative or an ally. The first time occurred during the <a href="/wiki/Loguetown_Arc" title="Loguetown Arc">Loguetown Arc</a> with <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Dragon" title="Monkey D. Dragon">Monkey D. Dragon</a>; the second time occurred during the <a href="/wiki/Arabasta_Arc" title="Arabasta Arc">Arabasta Arc</a> with <a href="/wiki/Portgas_D._Ace" title="Portgas D. Ace">Portgas D. Ace</a>; and the third time during the <a href="/wiki/Marineford_Arc" title="Marineford Arc">Marineford Arc</a> with <a href="/wiki/Boa_Hancock" title="Boa Hancock">Boa Hancock</a>.
<ul><li>These instances are similar to how <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Garp" title="Monkey D. Garp">Monkey D. Garp</a> cornered <a href="/wiki/Gol_D._Roger" title="Gol D. Roger">Gol D. Roger</a> multiple times but was unable to capture him.</li>
<li>It can be said that Smoker and Luffy have a cat-and-mouse relationship, with Smoker always chasing Luffy whenever they encounter each other.</li></ul></li>
<li>In the 2nd, 3rd, 4th, 5th, 6th and 7th <a href="/wiki/Popularity_Polls" title="Popularity Polls">fan polls</a> of most popular characters, Smoker was ranked 12th, 14th, 20th, 24th, 33rd and 27th, respectively.
<ul><li>In the 2nd and 3rd polls, Smoker is ranked as the most popular Marine; in the 4th, 5th, and 7th polls, he is the second most popular Marine after being overthrown in the first two cases by <a href="/wiki/Kuzan" title="Kuzan">Aokiji</a> and <a href="/wiki/Donquixote_Rosinante" title="Donquixote Rosinante">Donquixote Rosinante</a>; and in the 6th poll, he is ranked the third most popular Marine, ranked behind Donquixote Rosinante and again Aokiji.</li></ul></li>
<li>Along with <a href="/wiki/Tashigi" title="Tashigi">Tashigi</a>, Smoker has appeared in more sections of the overall storyline than any other character outside the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a>, making at least token appearances in all except the <a href="/wiki/Sky_Island_Saga" title="Sky Island Saga">Sky Island</a>, <a href="/wiki/Thriller_Bark_Saga" title="Thriller Bark Saga">Thriller Bark</a>, <a href="/wiki/Whole_Cake_Island_Saga" title="Whole Cake Island Saga">Whole Cake Island</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Wano_Country_Saga" title="Wano Country Saga">Wano Country</a> sagas.</li>
<li>In the spin-off manga <i><a href="/wiki/One_Piece:_Kobiyama_Who_Looks_Like_Koby_-_Two_Piece_in_a_Pod" title="One Piece: Kobiyama Who Looks Like Koby - Two Piece in a Pod">One Piece: Kobiyama Who Looks Like Koby - Two Piece in a Pod</a></i>, one of the characters, Sumoshige, is a high school student who resembles Smoker.</li>
<li>Smoker's favorite food is smoked <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chicken_as_food" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Chicken as food">chicken</a>, a reference to his Devil Fruit's abilities.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_5-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="SBS-Based_Trivia">SBS-Based Trivia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSmoker%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D53&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li>Smoker's birthday, March 14, in Japan is known as '<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/White_Day" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:White Day">White Day</a>'<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">ホワイトデー</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Howaitodē</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>, a reference to his Devil Fruit's abilities (alluding to the "white" theme in all his attack names).<sup id="cite_ref-sbs27_6-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sbs27-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Smoker's hobbies are <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Casino" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Casino">casino</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ceramic_art" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Ceramic art">ceramic art</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
